<div id="review_1453395315" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1453395315" />
    <a title="Gavin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8192509-gavin"><img alt="Gavin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1338207884p2/8192509.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1453395315?book_show_action=true">Nov 27, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Gavin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Gavin" href="/user/show/8192509-gavin">Gavin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8192509-gavin?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1453395315" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4765302702651766861">This fourth instalment of the Night Huntress series was a bit of a mixed bag. It was still a fast paced and engaging read with the same blend of action, romance, humor, mystery that we have grown to expect from the series. It even had plenty of shock twists and turns that kept things quite intense, but was also riddled with a few annoying flaws. Some of Bones and Cat's behaviour was infuriating and it felt like Frost had dipped into the well once too often with some of her story arcs. <br/><br/>Cat and Bo</span>
  <span id="freeText4765302702651766861" style="display:none">This fourth instalment of the Night Huntress series was a bit of a mixed bag. It was still a fast paced and engaging read with the same blend of action, romance, humor, mystery that we have grown to expect from the series. It even had plenty of shock twists and turns that kept things quite intense, but was also riddled with a few annoying flaws. Some of Bones and Cat's behaviour was infuriating and it felt like Frost had dipped into the well once too often with some of her story arcs. <br /><br />Cat and Bones are trying to relax after the happenings at the end of the third book when it becomes apparent that poor Cat has caught they eye of yet another ancient undead sex pest. Gregor "the dream snatcher" has been invading Cat's dreams(the guy treats bedtime with the same sort of creepy glee as Edward Cullen) and is claiming that Cat is actually his wife rather than Bones wife and that Mencheries wiped the whole experience from Cat's memory. Crazy happenings ensue as the "no means yes" former school girl snatcher tries to drag Cat kicking and screaming to his bed! <br /><br />The plot was a little far fetched, but would not have been too bad if I had not reached the stage where I'm getting bored by the fact that every vamp that meets Cat thinks she is the hottest girl on the planet and simply has to have her no matter what the cost. It is like there are no other women in this world! <br /><br />Another real irritation was the behaviour of both Cat and Bones. Bones was an asshole at times to Cat even stormed off in a drama laden huff at one point. Cat was even worse as her loose moral code hit an all time low in this instalment. <br /><br />Despite my moaning I did still manage to enjoy this. Frost managed to keep my attention as the story moved along at a rapid pace. <br /><br />Rating: 3.5 stars. It might have been 4 if it had less irritating moments.<br /><br />Audio Note: Tavia Gilbert was awesome as always.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="4765302702651766861" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_458420978" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/458420978" />
    <a title="Carole (Carole&#39;s Random Life in Books)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books"><img alt="Carole (Carole&#39;s Random Life in Books)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1415550632p2/5892196.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/458420978?book_show_action=true">Nov 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carole (Carole&#39;s Random Life in Books)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carole (Carole&#39;s Random Life in Books)" href="/user/show/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books">Carole (Carole&#39;s Random Life in Books)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/32389591-destined-for-an-early-grave">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=2019">2019</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=series">series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer458420978" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3074058852442221114">This review can also be found at <a href='https://carolesrandomlife.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Carole's Random Life in Books</a>.<br/><br/>I am loving my re-read of this series! I loved this book when I first read it almost seven years ago and I loved the audiobook just as much now. I had planned to listen to something else but something made me put everything aside to spend a little bit of time with Cat and Bones. I am so glad that I listened to that little voice in my head that told me to forget my plans and listen to this book because it was exactly what I needed. <br/><br/>Th</span>
  <span id="freeText3074058852442221114" style="display:none">This review can also be found at <a href="https://carolesrandomlife.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Carole's Random Life in Books</a>.<br /><br />I am loving my re-read of this series! I loved this book when I first read it almost seven years ago and I loved the audiobook just as much now. I had planned to listen to something else but something made me put everything aside to spend a little bit of time with Cat and Bones. I am so glad that I listened to that little voice in my head that told me to forget my plans and listen to this book because it was exactly what I needed. <br /><br />This is the fourth book in a series that does need to be read in order since each book builds on the events of the previous installments. Cat and Bones were in a pretty good place at the start of this book. Things looked pretty calm but of course, that can't last for long. Cat and Bones have a small issue with Cat's ex that will be much more complicated than you could even imagine. <br /><br />I love the characters in this series. Cat and Bones are both awesome and I love them together. Vlad plays an important role in this book which was a big plus for me. Vlad is such an interesting character and I love his friendship with Cat. All of the key players from the series play a role in this story and there is a couple of nice additions as well. <br /><br />Tavia Gilbert does such a good job with this series. I adore the voice that she uses for Bones. It just feels so real to me. The dialogue in this story flowed absolutely wonderfully and I thought that she added a lot of emotion to this story. I loved the story when I read it on my kindle but there was something almost magical about experiencing it through the audiobook. <br /><br />I would highly recommend this series to others. This book was fantastic even with the unnecessary relationship drama. There were times that I wanted to shake the characters for their behavior but there was never a time that I wasn't enjoying myself so it doesn't even matter. I cannot wait to continue with my re-read.<br /><br /><b>Initial Thoughts</b><br />This book had a lot of unnecessary drama between Cat and Bones and there were times that I kind of wanted to shake them. It doesn't matter though because I loved this book. I really had a great time with it and I almost forgot how amazing Vlad is! Tavia Gilbert was phenomenal with her narration and I might have liked this book even more the second time around.<br /><br />Book Source: Audible purchase</span>

          </span>

<div id="review_154415141" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/154415141" />
    <a title="AngelLeah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5128064-angelleah"><img alt="AngelLeah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1427501935p2/5128064.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/154415141?book_show_action=true">Mar 14, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AngelLeah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AngelLeah" href="/user/show/5128064-angelleah">AngelLeah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer154415141" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14747723408872746949">I feel like I should write two reviews for this, one for the majority of the book and one for the ending. <br/><br/>Catherine (Cat) Crawfield started out as a bad-ass, tough woman; who was an intelligent, take-charge leader. Unfortunately, somewhere along the way we lost that character. Through the majority of "Destined for an Early Grave", the 4th book in the Night Huntress series, the reader is forced to listen to the inner dialogue of a woman with a very low self-esteem. When did Cat become this woman?</span>
  <span id="freeText14747723408872746949" style="display:none">I feel like I should write two reviews for this, one for the majority of the book and one for the ending. <br /><br />Catherine (Cat) Crawfield started out as a bad-ass, tough woman; who was an intelligent, take-charge leader. Unfortunately, somewhere along the way we lost that character. Through the majority of "Destined for an Early Grave", the 4th book in the Night Huntress series, the reader is forced to listen to the inner dialogue of a woman with a very low self-esteem. When did Cat become this woman?! <br /><br />Have you ever had a female friend who would sit around and whine about the horrible problems in her relationship, while blaming everything on herself? Didn't you just want to scream and slap your friend to wake her up?! Are you really going to let him treat you like that?! Are you going to sit back and cry over losing him while he treats you like a doormat?! <br /><br />Of course, if this book wasn't written from only Cat's point of view, then we might have known that her love, "Bones" was not the total jerk that we thought he might be. That is a serious downside when writing a book from only one viewpoint. Unfortunately, it ruined this book for me. I spent too much time pissed off at Bones and couldn't really enjoy the book. Although there was an apology, Cat never actually demanded one. Instead, she was willing to move on without even getting one. <br /><br />hhhmmm.... keep secrets from me, treat me like a child, flip out when I do what I think is best with the limited information that I have, break my heart, publicly humiliate me.... oh, but since I have some of the blame in it, I'll just forget your part and beg for your forgiveness. *puke*<br /><br />The action in this book was fantastic. The other characters are always intriguing and I'm glad to see that some books have been written about them. The ending was good. Maybe the next book will have Cat back to her kick-ass, smart, independent self. I missed her in this book.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14747723408872746949" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText14815873920453677751" style="display:none"><b> 3 ☆ Vampire telenovela</b><br /><br />Bound in vampire marriage to Bones at the end of book #2 and engaged human-style at the beginning of book #3, Cat and Bones' relationship appears solid. Known as the Dreamsnatcher, Gregor can take away anyone once he touches them during their dreams. He doesn't hold back since asserting that he and Cat were bound in vampiric matrimony 10 years earlier.         <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer13711774031670133277">4.5 This series gets better and better Stars<br/><br/>Out of the 4 books I have read, Destined for an early Grave is my favorite so far. Gah, this book had me twisted up!<br/><br/>I love Bones and Cat and I love how each book has a crazy storyline and the awesome couple has to overcome whatever is thrown their way.<br/><br/>In this book someone wants Cat and he claims that he is her TRUE (a.k.a. her first husband). He can walk into her dreams and she is no longer safe as she sleeps.<br/><br/>This book was probably the hardest book out</span>
  <span id="freeText13711774031670133277" style="display:none">4.5 This series gets better and better Stars<br /><br />Out of the 4 books I have read, Destined for an early Grave is my favorite so far. Gah, this book had me twisted up!<br /><br />I love Bones and Cat and I love how each book has a crazy storyline and the awesome couple has to overcome whatever is thrown their way.<br /><br />In this book someone wants Cat and he claims that he is her TRUE (a.k.a. her first husband). He can walk into her dreams and she is no longer safe as she sleeps.<br /><br />This book was probably the hardest book out of the series because Cat and Bones’ love is SUPER tested. I was glued to the pages and I didn’t want to stop reading because I didn’t know what was going to happen.<br /><br />Would Cat go to her other husband? How would Bones react? What does it mean for the perfect couple?<br /><br />I love how each book the relationship between Cat and Bones progresses. Gah. I can’t get over this series and now I need to read the Spin-off with Charles! <br /><br /> <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13711774031670133277" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_824721181" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/824721181" />
    <a title="Didi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6082482-didi"><img alt="Didi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459297426p2/6082482.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/824721181?book_show_action=true">Jan 15, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Didi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Didi" href="/user/show/6082482-didi">Didi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=angst-in-my-pants">angst-in-my-pants</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=my-vampire-lover">my-vampire-lover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer824721181" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8850541847298061243">This series is fantastic! I'm hurdling towards the end, gaining on the seventh book that ends this series and ends my voyeuristic adventures with Bones and Cat. Those two sure got a beating this time around! This book was definitely more angsty than the previous ones. Bones and Cat suffered through some seriously turbulent times, even separating for a while that left me bereft and empty. I had to sneak a peak farther into the book to appease my heartbreak--I don't like to cheat, but I honestly n</span>
  <span id="freeText8850541847298061243" style="display:none">This series is fantastic! I'm hurdling towards the end, gaining on the seventh book that ends this series and ends my voyeuristic adventures with Bones and Cat. Those two sure got a beating this time around! This book was definitely more angsty than the previous ones. Bones and Cat suffered through some seriously turbulent times, even separating for a while that left me bereft and empty. I had to sneak a peak farther into the book to appease my heartbreak--I don't like to cheat, but I honestly needed to know when to expect some making up!<br /><br />From the beginning our fearless couple dealt with some gut-wrenching revelations, the biggest being Cat previously making a blood bond(vampire marriage) with someone else. The problem is she doesn't have any recollection of this. So begins the action packed and stress inducing adventure in finding out what really happened. This situation causes a huge rift between Bones and Cat.<br />She's always been jealous of Bones' past and his many conquests. Her insecurity becomes a roaring fire and they both say hurtful and vicious things to each other. Bones has always suspected Cat of having one foot out the door, so to speak. He knows she loves him more than anything but the revelations that she may have been given to another tears him apart and brings his own insecurities to the forefront. <br /><br />Many readers had a problem with this book specifically because of the rift between our beloved couple. I can see that but more importantly I see it a different way. All couples fight, viciously even at times, but it's how we emerge from these differences that determines the strength of our relationships. The same for Bones and Cat. They have always faced hurdles to their relationship but nothing that acutely threatens it, till now. I think they had to go through this in order to push the boundaries of being together, to see that their love is truly iron-clad. <br /><br />I'm not trying to pick sides, but Cat seemed to annoy me with her actions rather than Bones. She's often impulsive for her own good and used her insecurities as a crutch with him. She acts without knowing all the angles and doubts Bones's abilities more than he doubts hers. There were many situations that required the simple task of ASKING A QUESTION. she succumbed to her own fears and denied her instincts. There's a scene when Bones confronts Cat about their troubled relationship that killed me. It was excruciating to read and imagine how he felt saying the things he did. My heart broke for both of them but I have never seen Bones so raw and hurting, it almost did me in.<br /><br />Not to say that Bones was innocent. He was responsible for holding back information and acting before ASKING A QUESTION. It got to the point that the stubbornness these two shared was keeping them apart. But like I said, their strength and love for one another is unbreakable. Many things happen here, including a new development that completely surprised everyone and although things ended beautifully between Cat and Bones, there are many unresolved issues looming on the horizon and enemies waiting in the midst. <br />Looking forward to continuing this series, it's an excellent one giving us everything from action to hot romance!</span>
  <a data-text-id="8850541847298061243" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_75131283" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/75131283" />
    <a title="Rane" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1987431-rane"><img alt="Rane" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1419878997p2/1987431.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/75131283?book_show_action=true">Oct 20, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rane" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rane" href="/user/show/1987431-rane">Rane</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1987431-rane?shelf=paranormal-pnr-supernatural">paranormal-pnr-supernatural</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer75131283" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5338549590763473042"> <i> Cat and her undead vampire lover Bones are taking an long overdue holiday, to finally get away from the fighting and trouble that has filled their lives of late, that is until Cat starts to dream of a vampire whom wants her and will do anything to have her!</i><br/><br/><br/> Jeaniene Frost strikes another out of the ballpark with Destined for an Early Grave, thinking by now her books would be somewhat lagging or dragging by now, not with Frost they don’t! This books pick up a few weeks later after At Grave’s En</span>
  <span id="freeText5338549590763473042" style="display:none"> <i> Cat and her undead vampire lover Bones are taking an long overdue holiday, to finally get away from the fighting and trouble that has filled their lives of late, that is until Cat starts to dream of a vampire whom wants her and will do anything to have her!</i><br /><br /><br /> Jeaniene Frost strikes another out of the ballpark with Destined for an Early Grave, thinking by now her books would be somewhat lagging or dragging by now, not with Frost they don’t! This books pick up a few weeks later after At Grave’s End, with Cat and Bones trying to take it easy, no such luck when Cat starts having dreams of a vampire whom claims to be her vampire husband! Then when all hell breaks loose Cat and Bones must not only face off with this new baddie but comes to terms with each other.<br /><br /> While romance was on a break with Grave’s End, this time around romance takes center stage as things come to head between Cat and Bones. Always fighting, with no rest in between, Cat and Bones have a lot to deal with when it comes to their relationship and trust issues.. This has been building for awhile between the pair and does it explored in all it’s fire and glory and not in a good way either. <br /> Which brought me to my overall rating score, while I adore this series to bits this time around I was ready to rip my hair out over Cat and Bones arguments and disagreements and misunderstandings. I wanted to shake them hoping it would knock some sense into them! But thinking about relationships, their not all happyhappy or perfect and are not without their major bumps in the road and that’s what Cat and Bones have to overcome this time around with the air finally clean between them and the walls coming down. <br /><br /> This also gave a chance for other secondary characters to shine as Bones and Cat deal with their troubles between each other. Making me a happy fangirl, we see another side of Spade whose caring and protective (and funny and can overreact) of his love ones and willing to go the extra mile to help. It made me love him more and now I can’t wait for his story! One whom took me by surprise was Vald who was another who helped Cat through her tough time, he was also really funny with his comments toward the events going on. <br /><br /> This book was really full of twists and turns and surprises in the overall story, making me wonder how things will turn out later for the said characters....<br /><br />Overall: with romance back in the driver seat along with action, I really enjoyed this book that was full of a lot of surprises for the reader</span>
  <a data-text-id="5338549590763473042" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_147743886" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/147743886" />
    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4281149-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1491245473p2/4281149.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/147743886?book_show_action=true">Feb 12, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura" href="/user/show/4281149-laura">Laura</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4281149-laura?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4281149-laura?shelf=scorching-hot">scorching-hot</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer147743886" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7904090308996398755">Contrary to other readers of this book, this was my favorite out of the whole Night Huntress series! I loved every minute of it from start to finish and I was cursing myself when I finished it because it was over. <br/>One of my favorite things about the whole book was that, for the first time, Bones had a little “competition” for Cat. Throughout their relationship to date, Cat had nothing compared to the history that Bones had and I found it rather entertaining that he felt so threatened by Gregor.<br/>O</span>
  <span id="freeText7904090308996398755" style="display:none">Contrary to other readers of this book, this was my favorite out of the whole Night Huntress series! I loved every minute of it from start to finish and I was cursing myself when I finished it because it was over. <br />One of my favorite things about the whole book was that, for the first time, Bones had a little “competition” for Cat. Throughout their relationship to date, Cat had nothing compared to the history that Bones had and I found it rather entertaining that he felt so threatened by Gregor.<br />One of my least favorite things, but I think it added it to the reasons I liked it (I know I am weird, I know), was how big of a JERK Bones was. This behavior is very typical of men when they feel threatened, however, I thought Bones pushed it way over the top and, at times, I just wanted to smack the $* out of him! Then, when Cat was informed that Bones was not grieving over her, but getting along just fine, I wanted to hurl the book across the room.<br />I am glad I didn’t throw it across the room so that I could read the incredibly HOT, HOT, HOT, make up sex scene, that seriously, had me so turned on, I wanted a cigarette, and I don’t even smoke! One of the hottest scene’s EVER, in my opinion.<br />Most of all, I thought that this book was extremely intense. I loved the fact that I was on the edge of my seat the entire time whether it was from the action scenes, the love scenes, the lover’s quarrel’s, etc. I LOVED IT! I also was so glad to read more about one of my favorite character’s Vlad, and I loved how he stood by Cat’s side even when there was trouble in paradise!<br />This book, like the three before, was full of my favorite one liners and fantastic dialog and humor. I adore Jeaniene Frost!! <br />FIVE + HUGE STARS!!!!!!!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7904090308996398755" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('1uyFyO6EWIaWbAHlIPAb71TCm75iCUTN9o1J/eXITTb3J/wOf4P2JBO0q6gKuz+oNKFLEBZ0PazFB6O8yanScw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Gtyit/PH5B0N7pUnfxGRl5jqcjfo8dN3s8RXzKMwq2M7F9txYsBKv4g2P2pVWrXQ+ImimZyMqhaATr2Nj1E0Jg==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer3202146584148947944">Jeaniene Frost is the New York Times, USA Today, and international bestselling author of the Night Huntress series, the Night Prince series, the Broken Destiny series, and the new Night Rebel series. To date, foreign rights for her novels have sold to twenty different countries. Jeaniene lives in Florida with her husband Matthew, who long ago accepted that she rarely cooks and always sleeps in on </span>
  <span id="freeText3202146584148947944" style="display:none">Jeaniene Frost is the New York Times, USA Today, and international bestselling author of the Night Huntress series, the Night Prince series, the Broken Destiny series, and the new Night Rebel series. To date, foreign rights for her novels have sold to twenty different countries. Jeaniene lives in Florida with her husband Matthew, who long ago accepted that she rarely cooks and always sleeps in on the weekends. Aside from writing, Jeaniene enjoys reading, poetry, watching movies with her husband, exploring old cemeteries, spelunking and traveling – by car. Airplanes, children, and cook books frighten her.<br /><br />For information on Jeaniene's books, book trailers, deleted scenes, creature mythology, and more, please visit: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.jeanienefrost.com">www.jeanienefrost.com</a><br /></span>
